# Tangerine ERP Рђћ Live Build Progress

> **Single source of truth for "% complete."** Update this doc whenever a phase or module lands (it's part of the PR, like the user-guide chapters). Roadmap: `project-erp-build-roadmap` memory + `docs/tangerine/` arch docs. 25 phases (P1РђЊP25), 49 modules (M1РђЊM49), 7 pre-existing apps (E1РђЊE7). **The 3 pre-existing operational apps that feed Tangerine Рђћ ATS, PO WIP (Tanda), Inventory Planning Рђћ are documented in [`docs/apps/`](../apps/README.md).**

**Last updated:** 2026-07-15 (#1813 **Universal Totals button Рђћ total any column with numbers** (CEO: *"add a Totals button to total any column with numbers"*). New shared **`<TotalsButton>`** (`src/tanda/exports/TotalsButton.tsx`) toggles a compact totals strip that sums every numeric column over the CURRENT filtered/visible rows Рђћ money columns (TRUE cents) render **$X.XX**, qty/number columns render with thousands separators, **percentage columns are NOT summed** (averaging % misleads Рєњ left blank with a footnote), text/date columns blank. Rides the **existing universal ExportButton pattern**: rather than hand-wiring ~146 panels, `<ExportButton>` now renders `<TotalsButton>` beside itself using the SAME `rows`/`columns` props, so **every export control app-wide gains totals for free** Рђћ opt out with the new `noTotals` prop. TotalsButton **auto-hides** on tables with no numeric columns (master-data/text grids) and is **opted OUT** on statement-shaped reports whose exported rows embed subtotal/total lines (**Balance Sheet, Trial Balance, Cash Flow, Segment P&L**; Income Statement uses its own statement export button) to avoid double-counting; matrix/transaction-list grids keep it. Pure logic in `src/tanda/exports/tableTotals.ts` (`computeColumnTotals` sums cents raw, `formatIsSummable`, conservative `inferredNumeric` Рђћ never sums numeric-looking strings/codes). 16 vitest (cents/null-skip/percent-skip/inferred detection); typecheck 0-new, vite green. Dark styling, subtle distinct totals row, no decorative emoji. user-guide ch18.) ┬и (#1810 **Inventory Aging Рђћ aged-date clarity + filter cleanup** (CEO: *"why are styles clearly aged >30d showing in the 0-30 column?"* + *"remove the Buckets window and Style/Color/Size fields, they do nothing"*). **NOT a bucketing bug** Рђћ verified 0 mis-bucketed rows at today's as-of; the screenshot was **aged to 06/30** (its 585d-oldest vs today's 600d = exactly 15 days back), where stock received 05/31 genuinely IS РЅц30 days old Рєњ lands in 0-30 (reproduced RBB1438NFL to the cent: at 06/30 b1=$473.60/wavg 174d/oldest 585d = the screenshot; at today b1=$0). Root cause = **age buckets are measured from the Aged date, not today**, and the aged date wasn't obvious. Fix: when aged date РЅа today, the toolbar shows an **amber "Aged as of MM/DD/YYYY Рђћ not today" pill + "Use today" button**; else "aged as of today". **Removed** the confusing **custom Buckets cut-offs input** (now fixed 30/60/90/180/365) and the **Style code / Color / Size text filters** (search box + dropdowns remain); endpoints still accept the params (harmless). No RPC/migration change; tsc/eslint/vite clean. user-guide ch11 ┬Д11.4c.) ┬и (#1805 **Inventory Aging Рђћ nightly cost-refresh cron** (CEO: *"yes do it"* to a nightly so new receipts don't re-accumulate uncosted). Tier 2 = estimate (flagged by `source_ref='style_sibling_avg:<style>'`, reversible); applied on CEO review. Residual truly-uncosted stays honestly flagged (qty/ages always exact). user-guide ch11 ┬Д11.4c. Рџа№ИЈprobe path: cost lives on native `purchase_order_lines` (50% of items) + Xoro `tanda_pos.data->Items[].UnitPrice`; `ip_item_avg_cost` was only 288 manual rows.) ┬и (#1801 **Inventory Aging Рђћ ATS last-received for mirrored stock + effective cost + Uncosted flag** (CEO follow-up to #1797: *"incorporate the ATS last-received date for mirrored styles only"* + *"how do we deal with the wide zero-cost issue"*). Root-caused with prod probes: mirrored on-hand (`source_kind='xoro_rest_size'`, ~7.5k items) is a single snapshot layer dated to the sync, so every size shared one meaningless age; and **4,061 layers / 464k units are $0-cost** Рђћ only ~2% fixable from any cost table (the rest have NO cost anywhere, e.g. RYB0412B Cali Bear Рђћ a genuine data gap, not a join bug; RYB0412-BLACK *is* costed at $5.71). Migration `20261110000000` (applied+prod-verified): recreates `inventory_aging_report`/`inventory_aging_kpis` and adds `inventory_aging_layers` (drill) so all three share one logic. **Effective received date (MIRRORED layers only)**: age off `COALESCE(ats_last_receipt, MAX(ip_receipts_history.received_date), snapshot date)` clamped at as-of Рђћ the same last-received basis ATS uses; **Tangerine-received layers (ap_receipt/receipt/transfer/native PO) keep their true `received_at`**. New `ats_last_receipt` table (size-grain, keyed by `sku_code` so it joins the size-grain layer Рђћ the ATS 'manual' snapshot is style-color grain and would NOT join) populated by planning-sync's ATS step from the raw pre-aggregation feed rows (future dates clamped, MAX per sku). **Effective cost**: `COALESCE(layer cents, avg_cost├Ќ100, item unit_cost├Ќ100, 0)`; still-$0 units roll into a new **`uncosted_qty`** output Рђћ surfaced as an **Uncosted KPI tile + amber per-row badge + export column**, and **excluded from $ totals** so $0 reads "no cost on file" not "worth $0" (**qty/ages always exact**). Result for RYB0412: ages now spread 0-30/31-60/91-180 (oldest 58Рєњ119d), value ~$0Рєњ**$9,829.85**, 10,109 units flagged uncosted; entity-wide **oldest 682d, dead-stock $52,649, uncosted 455,726 units** now visible (were masked). Drill shows effective date (raw snapshot in tooltip) + **(mirrored)** tag + per-layer uncosted. Cost back-fill from PO/receipt lines = separate data pass. user-guide ch11 ┬Д11.4c.) ┬и (**Inventory Aging Рђћ best-in-class aged-inventory report** (CEO: *"add a best-in-class inventory aging report, multiple filters including aged date; the ATS aging report is good but Tangerine needs to be richer"*). New `­ЪЊд Inventory Рєњ РЈ│ Inventory Aging` panel (route `?m=inventory_aging`, RBAC analytics, READ-ONLY). **Richer than ATS**: where the ATS aged-inventory report ages a whole style off ONE "last received date" always to today, this ages **true FIFO layers** (`inventory_layers.received_at`) as of **any chosen aged date** Рђћ each layer's on-hand lands in the bucket for *its own* age. Migration `20261090000000` (applied+prod-verified) adds `inventory_aging_report(...)` (per-grain aggregate: on-hand qty, cost value, weighted-avg age, oldest, qty+$ across 6 configurable buckets, carrying cost, velocity) + `inventory_aging_kpis(...)` (headline totals + per-bucket + dead stock) + supporting indexes. **Carrying-cost economics kept 1:1 with ATS** (`src/lib/inventoryAging.ts`): interest 9%/yr (daily=val├Ќrate/360), storage $20/pallet-month at 864 pcs/pallet Рђћ unit-tested for centsРєћdollars parity with the ATS `calcAgedCosts`. **Filters**: aged-date picker + presets (Today/Month-end/Quarter-end/Year-end/Рѕњ30/Рѕњ90/Рѕњ180d), group-by (style / style+color / SKU / category / warehouse / vendor), configurable bucket cut-offs, category/brand/vendor/warehouse/gender/style/color/size, min-age (layer-level), single-bucket, slow-movers (no sale РЅЦ N days incl never-sold), min-$ / min-qty (group HAVING), include-zero. **UI**: KPI header (on-hand value, wavg age, SKUs/styles, dead stock, annual carry) + bucket-distribution strip; grid with per-bucket $ (stale buckets amber), carry %/yr + $/yr, velocity (days-since-sale, weeks-of-supply); **full-row click Рєњ per-grain FIFO-layer drill** (each layer's received date, age, source, warehouse, on-hand, unit cost, value); universal ExportButton. Endpoints `/api/internal/inventory-aging/{report,filters,layers}`. As-of caveat documented (ages the receipt date against *current* remaining_qty Рђћ not a full point-in-time restatement, matching ATS on-hand semantics). Registered in the menuKeys dual-registry + erp/modules + tangerineModules. 15 vitest green; tsc/eslint/vite clean. user-guide ch11 ┬Д11.4c.) ┬и **Today router + brief staleness** Рђћ two changes to the assistant-first Today page. (1) The greeting-bar **"What do you want to work on?"** field is now a pure **intent ROUTER, not a chat**: a new pure resolver `src/tanda/todayIntentRouter.ts` (`resolveIntent`) matches the typed phrase against the operator's **live to-dos** (title/pack/panel + synonym map), routable suggestions, and the full module list, scoring strong identifier hits ├Ќ3 + word overlap ├Ќ1 with a per-kind tie-break that prefers a live TO-DO over a bare module Рђћ so *"pos flagged here"* opens the flagged-PO to-do, *"month close"* Рєњ Month-End Close, *"chargebacks"* Рєњ Chargebacks. Confident match navigates (`openItem`/`goToPanel`) + `notify` toast; ambiguous Рєњ inline **Did you mean:** chips; no match Рєњ gentle hint. The floating Рюе Ask AI button stays the Q&A surface (`askAI` removed from this field). (2) The morning **brief no longer contradicts the live process cards**: `brief.js` now compares a CACHED brief's `source_json.processes` states to the live aggregate via new pure `processStatesDiverged(cached, live)` and regenerates on a **state flip** (e.g. a Xoro mirror errorРєњok) Рђћ NOT on count drift Рђћ best-effort (any throw falls back to the cached brief). Tests: `src/tanda/__tests__/todayIntentRouter.test.ts` + `api/_lib/assistant/__tests__/brief-staleness.test.js` (14 new; 825 assistant/tanda tests green). Guide ch46.) ┬и 2026-07-14 (#1786 **On-hand single-source PR1: Xoro by-size Рєњ planning snapshot** (Inventory Planning) Рђћ first step of the on-hand single-source-of-truth plan (docs/tangerine/onhand-single-source-of-truth.md). New `rollUpXoroOnHandToSnapshot` + `POST /api/planning/sync-onhand-xoro` re-source the Xoro REST by-size on-hand (`tangerine_size_onhand`, the truth, per warehouse) into `ip_inventory_snapshot` as **source='tangerine'**, item_idРєњsku_id identity (both size-grain, same master), warehouses + native PPK grain + zero rows preserved. **ADDITIVE**: the default 'xoro' reader filters `source!=tangerine`, so live wholesale runs are untouched; the Tangerine supply source now reflects the by-size Xoro truth. Backfilled + tied out to the UNIT (985,898 units / 6,816 rows / 4 warehouses). 22 planning-sync tests. Reader flip + Excel-path deprecation are follow-on PRs) ┬и 2026-07-14 (#1777 **Sync Health false 'stale' on open-PO feed** Рђћ the panel flagged `open_pos_planning` (Open POs Рєњ planning supply) as stale 96.9h, reading as a mirror failure. It was a FALSE alarm: the open-PO nightly (`post_purchase_orders.py` Step 2 Рєњ `syncOpenPosFromTandaPos`) runs fine (log `step2 upserted:818`) but upserted `ip_open_purchase_orders` WITHOUT setting `last_seen_at`, so that column only ever got its INSERT default and never advanced for unchanged PO lines Рђћ and `v_xoro_feed_health` uses `max(last_seen_at)` as its freshness proxy. The open-SOs sibling already stamps `last_seen_at=syncStartedAt` every run (why `open_sos_planning` reads fresh); this adds the missing twin (7-line change; stale-prune keys off `source_line_key`, unaffected). Current false-red cleared in prod (bumped the 818 current open-PO lines' `last_seen_at`). Found while checking Sync Health after the SO fix below.)
**Last updated:** 2026-07-15 (#1814 **AR Invoices Рђћ grid columns + draft warnings + ship-to/terms auto-populate + search-anything** (CEO batch of 5). (6) **Grid columns**: added **Payment Terms** (`payment_terms.code`), **Due Date**, **Payment Date** (newest non-void receipt applied via `ar_receipt_applications`Рєњ`ar_receipts.receipt_date`), and **Credit Applied** Рђћ the operator's "Vendor Credit"; in AR the real data is **customer credit memos that reverse this invoice** (`ar_invoices.reverses_invoice_id`), summed over posted memos, so the column is honestly labelled *Credit Applied* (shown negative/green). Existing **Balance** column already IS the "Invoice Balance" (`totalРѕњpaid`, does NOT net credit memos Рђћ they are separate docs). All server-derived in the list handler (`enrichInvoiceRows`, best-effort per-column), sortable, column-prefs toggle, added to the ExportButton. (7) **Draft warnings** via the shared warn UI: saving with **no customer** warns and blocks; a line carrying qty but **$0 sales price** raises a warn-and-confirm (mirrors the SO missing-price guard, `getDocumentData()`). (8) **Ship-to auto-populate**: on customer select the default (else first) `customer_locations` row auto-fills, and a toast warns when the customer has **>1** ship-to. (9) **Payment terms auto-populate** from `customers.payment_terms_id` on customer select, and **Due Date auto-computed** as invoice date + `payment_terms.due_days` Рђћ *fixed a latent bug: the effect read `net_days` (undefined) so it never fired* Рђћ recomputes on terms/date change but never clobbers a hand-edited due date (`dueDateEdited` flag; pure `computeDueDate` in `src/tanda/arDueDate.ts`, 7 vitest). (10) **Search** broadened from invoice-# only to **search-anything** server-side: invoice #, customer name/code, line SKU/style/description, status, and amount Рђћ pre-resolves customer + line matches to id lists then one indexed `.or(...)`. **No migration** (all columns/tables exist). tsc ratchet 0-new, vite + vitest + check:api green. user-guide ch16.) ┬и (#1810 **Inventory Aging Рђћ aged-date clarity + filter cleanup** (CEO: *"why are styles clearly aged >30d showing in the 0-30 column?"* + *"remove the Buckets window and Style/Color/Size fields, they do nothing"*). **NOT a bucketing bug** Рђћ verified 0 mis-bucketed rows at today's as-of; the screenshot was **aged to 06/30** (its 585d-oldest vs today's 600d = exactly 15 days back), where stock received 05/31 genuinely IS РЅц30 days old Рєњ lands in 0-30 (reproduced RBB1438NFL to the cent: at 06/30 b1=$473.60/wavg 174d/oldest 585d = the screenshot; at today b1=$0). The assistant graduates to DOING: a looped `run_action` tool whose executor only ever calls a pack action's read-only `preview()` (never a write); draft/write_confirm modes return a preview + an HMAC confirmation token (reusing the appJwt primitive) that binds {action, sha256(commit_payload), auth_user_id, entity_id, jti, exp}; the model relays it as a terminal present_confirmation card on the EXISTING actions[] channel. **The write boundary is a SEPARATE authenticated endpoint** `POST /api/internal/assistant/actions/confirm` (NOT a re-invocation of the same-origin-only ask-grid loop that trusts body.user_id Рђћ the load-bearing correction to parent ┬Д6): it authenticates a real identity, verifies the token, re-checks RBAC authoritatively via loadEffectivePermissions, re-hashes to guarantee preview==commit, then calls action.commit(). **Last updated:** 2026-07-14 (#1748 **Off-provider encrypted DB backups** (DR) Рђћ closes the audit gap where every prod copy (PITR + wal-g) lived inside Supabase: a provider-level loss would take all of them at once. New GitHub Actions workflow `.github/workflows/db-backup.yml` runs nightly (08:30 UTC, after the overnight Xoro + recon crons) + on-demand (`workflow_dispatch`): `pg_dump -Fc` of the prod **public** schema via the IPv4 session-mode Supavisor pooler (`aws-1-us-west-1.pooler.supabase.com:5432` Рђћ GitHub runners are IPv4-only, so the direct IPv6 `db.<ref>` host is unusable; port 6543 transaction mode can't run pg_dump), then `openssl` AES-256-CBC (pbkdf2 200k) symmetric-encrypt with the `BACKUP_PASSPHRASE` secret, then **self-verify** every run (decrypt + `pg_restore --list`, fail loudly if unreadable or < 50 table-data sections), then upload as a 30-day GitHub artifact Рђћ living **off Supabase** (GitHub = different blast radius). On failure: loud `::error::` + best-effort `app_errors(source='cron', fingerprint=cron:db-backup:failure)` breadcrumb. Storage probed 2026-07-14: prod 5383 MB (3753 heap + 1080 idx) Рєњ `-Fc` dump ~0.7РђЊ1.2 GB/night, ~25РђЊ35 GB at 30-day retention (tunable via dispatch input; R2/B2 offload documented as the indefinite-retention upgrade). pg_dump 17 installed from PGDG to match the PG 17.6 server. Runs on existing `SUPABASE_DB_PASSWORD`/`SUPABASE_PROJECT_REF` secrets (no manual connection-string step); new secrets `BACKUP_PASSPHRASE` (**the sole recovery key Рђћ also saved off-GitHub**) + `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` set. Restore drill + full provider-loss recovery: `scripts/backup/restore-drill.md`; rationale/RPO-RTO: `scripts/backup/README.md`; DR-RUNBOOK gap marked CLOSED. |---|---|---|---|
| **Phases / slots (P1РђЊP25)** | **14 code-complete** (P1РђЊP10, P12, **P13** build+GL, P15, P16) + **9 MVP/­ЪЪА** (P11, P17РђЊP22, P24, P25); only **P23** (Xoro cutover, operator-gated) + the P14 PLM-ext slot remain Ргю (RBAC filled P14). Weighted by scope **РЅѕ78%**; 14/25 fully shipped = 56% | 25 | **~78%** |
| **Modules (M1РђЊM49 + РъЋM50)** | ~43 + РъЋM50; prior set + **M23 Returns/RMA ┬и M49 Drop-ship ┬и M13 3PL ┬и M14 EDI (surfaced) ┬и M9 reporting hub ┬и M20 1099 ┬и M21 Fixed Assets ┬и M22 Budgets**; remaining: M15 Public API, M19 Sales Tax, M46 BI charts, M32/M33 PLM-ext | 49 (+ins) | **~78%** |
| **Path to Xoro retirement (P1РђЊP23)** | through P12 + P14/P15 + P16 core + P18 portal + **P13 build+GL complete** + P17 planning surfaced + P19РђЊP22 MVPs; **P23 cutover itself = 0%** (operator parallel-run, first gate Cash ~2026-07-28) | 23 | **~78%** |

> Note: the **P14/P15 slots** hold operator insertions (RBAC, Brand Master), not the original roadmap scope (PLM-ext, Pricing Рђћ deferred). The brand / allocation / partition work is **built but GATED** (`BRAND_SCOPE_MODE` off) Рђћ shipped code, not yet *enforced* in prod.

> **Two important caveats when reading the %:**
> 1. **The done half is the hard half** Рђћ full dual-basis (accrual+cash) accounting, FIFO inventory, 5-yr AR backfill, close/financials, bank recon, and all three revenue integrations. Remaining phases are more numerous but individually lighter.
> 2. **Code РЅа Xoro off.** Retirement (P23) is gated by **calendar-floor parallel runs** Рђћ Tangerine must reconcile against Xoro within tolerance for ~2 consecutive months *per area* before each cutover. Actual retirement is paced by parallel-run verification, not just shipping code.

Legend: РюЁ done ┬и ­ЪЪА in progress / partial ┬и Ргю not started ┬и РъЋ operator insertion (off original numbering)

> - **3PL EDI transport made real (#1742)** Рђћ the X12 *engine* (940/850/820/997 builders + 944/945/846/997 parsers) already existed but nothing could transmit and no message ever moved. Migration `20260990000000` (applied prod + schema_migrations recorded) gives `tpl_providers` a full trading-partner profile Рђћ port, **encrypted** secret (`edi_secret_ciphertext`, AES-256-GCM via `api/_lib/crypto.js`, key `VENDOR_DATA_ENCRYPTION_KEY`; write-only, never returned), outbound/inbound/archive remote dirs, partner ISA qualifier+ID / GS ID (+ optional our-side overrides), `enabled_doc_types[]`, poll flag Рђћ and turns `edi_messages` into an **outbox/inbox state machine** (attempts, next_attempt_at backoff, last_error, file_name, group_control_number, ack_status; statuses gain failed/parsed/applied/staged; sets gain 846/944). Rewrote `transport.js` (encrypted-cred resolution w/ env-var fallback, connect/op **timeouts**, graceful no-creds queueing, `transmitEdi`/`testConnection`/`pollInbound`/`archiveInboundFile`) + new pure `outbox.js` (transitions, exp-backoff cap 6h, MAX_ATTEMPTS 5, dedupe) + `apply3pl.js` (997 **auto-reconciled** to the matching 940 by control number; 944/945/846 **STAGED for review**, never silently mutating shipments/inventory Рђћ and **nothing** ever posts to the GL). New tables `close_periods` (one per (entity, gl_period); status open Рєњ in_close Рєњ closed; entity default `coalesce(current_entity_id(), rof_entity_id())`; T10 `source` tagging; T11 `audit_row_changes` triggers; auth-only RLS) + `close_checklist_items` (unique `(close_period_id, item_key)`; kind auto|manual; status pending|pass|fail|signed_off; the numbers behind every verdict in `detail` jsonb; `signed_off_by/at` + required note). **8 automated checks** computed by the read-only SQL RPC `close_run_auto_checks(entity, period)` (all aggregation in SQL Рђћ no PostgREST caps; #1665 tie-out semantics): GL balanced per basis to the cent ┬и AR subledger tie 1105/1107/1108 ┬и AP 2000 tie (with the `pending_payments` waiver) ┬и bank/CC recon runs all `reconciled` ┬и no draft/unposted JEs ┬и 8007 Uncategorized activity = $0 ┬и factor statement Net OAR = GL 1107 as of period end (when a statement covers the month) ┬и revenue posted > $0. **6 manual sign-offs** (bank statements / factor statement / chargebacks / payroll / depreciation / controller) Рђћ note required, who/when recorded, revertible with reason while open. **Close period** requires ALL checks pass + ALL sign-offs, then locks `gl_periods` Рєњ `closed` through the audited `gl_period_transition_status` RPC (reason mandatory; `je_period_lock` triggers enforce); **Reopen** = admin-only + mandatory reason, checklist survives. > - **#1676 3-Way Match module (PO Рєћ receipt Рєћ AP bill)** Рђћ the classic apparel-ERP payables control, now bill-grain over the ENTIRE AP book. New engine `run_three_way_match()` (SQL RPC, set-based, idempotent Рђћ writes only `ap_bill_matches` verdicts, never GL/bills/POs): per bill it (a) finds POs via explicit `invoice_line_items.po_number` refs (the bills-register import carries them on merchandise bills) or a **fuzzy vendor+amount+date-window pass** (unique candidate only), (b) takes receiving evidence from `po_line_items.qty_received` (Xoro mirror) / `purchase_order_lines.qty_received` (native-only POs) Рђћ the standalone receipt tables are empty in prod, so PO-line received-qty IS the receipt leg, (c) computes price (bill avg unit price vs PO), qty (cumulative billed qty vs received) and amount (cumulative billed $ vs received $) variances against a **tolerance config table** (`ap_match_tolerances`: qty ┬▒2%, price ┬▒1% or $50, amount $100 Рђћ panel-editable). Statuses worst-wins: over_billed_vs_received / qty_variance / price_variance / no_po_found / matched_2way_po_only / matched_3way / not_applicable (vendor has no POs = expense/service bill). Nightly cron 06:45 UTC (after bank-mirror 05:30 + tie-out 06:00; `app_errors` source='cron'; notifies accounting on open over-billed). Panel: 3-Way Match gains a default **Bill Match Audit** tab (tiles by status with open-$ cut, filterable exception grid w/ seq-guard, per-PO evidence modal, View bill/PO drills, **Accept variance / Dispute with mandatory audit-logged reason** via `resolve_ap_bill_match` RPC + `set_audit_context` (T11); resolutions survive re-runs unless the verdict changes) Рђћ the original P13-C4 vendor-invoice staging flow lives on unchanged in a second tab. > - **#1638 PO modal matrix: render the sizes the order actually uses (off-scale + off-grain)** Рђћ a PO (ROF-P001265) rendered a **blank** size matrix for both `RBB0185` and `RBB0185-03SFPPK` even though the grid total was correct ($215,033.76 ties out). Two causes, one root: the modal considered only the style's *declared* sizes, not the sizes the order actually carries. (1) `RBB0185`'s size scale is **"Even Num Waist 28-42"** but the PO ordered **kids sizes 8/10/12/14** Рђћ the columns rendered (via the #1631 off-scale fix) but the locked-row **visibility filter** still used only the scale sizes, so every row (qty all off-scale) filtered away Рєњ blank. Fix: the filter (`entrySizes`) now uses the effective sizes (scale Рѕф actually-ordered). (2) `RBB0185-03SFPPK` has a prepack definition so it rendered a single **PPK48** column, but the order was cut at garment sizes 10/12/14 Рєњ the pack column had no qty. Fix: a new `ppActive` gate renders a style as a **prepack only when the order is at pack grain** (nothing entered yet, or a line at the pack token); a prepack-defined style ordered per size now renders as a normal size matrix. Applied to both the on-screen matrix AND `getDocumentData` (View Рєњ PDF/Excel). File: `src/tanda/LineMatrixBody.tsx`. No migration. Typecheck 0 new + build green + **9,672 tests pass**. User-guide ch28.

> - **#1637 PO grid Phase 4: ingest grain guardrail** Рђћ stops the grain-less-PPK-line class from re-entering at import (the class Phase 1 had to backfill). In `import-xoro-orders.mjs` `resolveSku`: when a PPK line finds **no sized pack row** but a **color-only** master row (size null Рђћ the "color-only rows stale" gap) exists for its colour, it now **binds to that row AND stamps the pack size** from the ItemNumber's `-PPKnn` token (guarded Рђћ never overwrites an existing sibling at that size). So a fresh import of a prepack style whose master carries only color-grain rows lands **grain-bearing** (per-each) instead of grain-less (which the grid read at pack grain, e.g. $127/each). Also: the `--apply` PO summary now prints an **ingest-guardrail nudge** to run `npm run audit:pos` after every import. Files: `scripts/import-xoro-orders.mjs`. No migration. `node --check` green. User-guide ch28.

> - **#1636 PO grid Phase 3: CI regression net + size-sort consolidation** Рђћ turns "green today" into "stays green". (1) **`npm run audit:pos`** Рђћ the read-only PO-grid audit is now a first-class command (schedule it alongside the nightly agents to catch DATA drift; exits non-zero on any invariant failure). (2) **CI logic gate** Рђћ new `api/_handlers/internal/purchase-orders/__tests__/grain-invariants.test.js` runs the audit's invariants (cost/PO-price ratio Рѕѕ [0.5,2], per-each plausibility, sane margin) over a **fixture of the exact prod shapes that broke** (P001177 pure-PPK, P001068 mixed garment+PPK, P001133 brand-list PPK, P001271 newly-linked) Рђћ a grain regression now **fails the build** (runs in the standard `vitest` CI). (3) **Size-sort consolidation** Рђћ `utils/tandaTypes.sizeSort` now **delegates to the shared `src/shared/sizeSort.ts` `compareSizes`**, so the PO WIP matrix + exports + row-detail all order sizes through ONE comparator (folds in the kids age-range fix from #1634); made numeric-first to preserve the frontend's tested convention. Verified against the **entire** suite: 9,672 tests pass. No migration. Typecheck 0 new + build green. User-guide ch28.

> - **#1635 PO grid Phase 1+2: unlinked-line backfill script + grain consolidation onto shared resolver** Рђћ closes the audit's remaining money/data reds. **Phase 1 (data, applied):** `scripts/backfills/link-ppk-prepack-lines.sql` (idempotent, committed for the record) linked the 6 unlinked POs' 21 SKU-less PPK lines to their catalog SKUs (positional Xoro-item match Рєњ unique normalized sku_code) AND set the pack **size** on the resolved color-only rows (from the Xoro `-PPKnn` token, collision-guarded) so grain resolves per-each Рђћ P001271 $127.20/pack Рєњ **$5.30/each**, not pack-grain. Audit ALL/SOME_UNLINKED 6Рєњ0. **Phase 2 (code, the real root):** `computePoLineMoney` now delegates the ambiguous-cost-grain decision to the **shared `resolvePerUnitCost` (`api/_lib/sales-grain.js`)** Рђћ the SAME resolver the sales COGS path already uses (`master cost > 2├Ќ the per-unit reference РЄњ per-pack ├и pack size`). Purchasing + sales now share **ONE grain resolver** instead of two divergent implementations (the anchor was a reinvention). Behavior-equivalent (10/10 tests unchanged); `packGrain` verdict still carried to SELL so cost + sell agree. Files: `api/_handlers/internal/purchase-orders/index.js`, `scripts/backfills/link-ppk-prepack-lines.sql` (new). No migration. Typecheck 0 new + build green + 10/10 tests. User-guide ch28.

> - **#1634 PO grid audit tool + canonical size-sort + prepack-label fix (Phase 0/B of the PO-grid audit)** Рђћ after ~30h of one-PO-at-a-time patching, shifted to **systematic audit**. (1) **`scripts/audit-pos.mjs`** Рђћ a read-only tool that runs all active POs through invariants (totals tie out, cost/grain sanity via the anchor, per-each plausibility, style-code case, description present, all/some-unlinked, PPK-without-prepack-def, unrecognized size) and prints a categorized failure report Рђћ the standing "prove it's zero" check. First run over 123 POs: **money math clean (totals/grain/case/plausibility all 0)**; remaining = 5 all-unlinked + 1 partial, 11 POs with PPK styles lacking prepack defs, 4 POs with kids age-range sizes. (2) **Canonical size sort** Рђћ new `src/shared/sizeSort.ts` (`compareSizes`, +5 tests) mirrors the backend `sizeSortKey`; handles kids **age-range** sizes (`XS(5-6)`, `S(7-8)`, `M(10-12)`) that a local `SIZE_RANK` map alpha-sorted into L,M,S,XL,XS. Row-detail now uses it. (3) **Prepack label** Рђћ the row-detail no longer shows "packs / PPK exploded" on **non-prepack** styles (CEO: "all carrots say prepack exploded"); shows "Qty" / "Unit $" unless the PO actually has PPK lines. Files: `scripts/audit-pos.mjs` (new), `src/shared/sizeSort.ts` (+test), `src/tanda/InternalPurchaseOrders.tsx`. No migration. Typecheck 0 new + build green + 5/5 tests. User-guide ch28.

> - **#1632 Canonical style_code on SKU creation (mis-cased REST-import codes stranded from their style)** Рђћ a PO (ROF-P000265) errored **"Style rbb0185 not found"** even though the style exists as **RBB0185** Рђћ because 37 `ip_item_master` rows carried the **lowercase** `rbb0185`, and `style_master` lookups are **case-sensitive**, so the size matrix couldn't resolve it. Root: a REST/import feed's mis-cased `BasePartNumber` was inherited verbatim onto new SKUs. Fix: `resolveOrCreateSku` (`api/_lib/styleMatrix.js`, the shared SKU-creation point for the ingest, build-orders, and the matrix resolve-sku endpoint) now takes the **canonical `style_code` from `style_master` by `style_id`** (authoritative) instead of the caller's string Рђћ a mis-cased feed code can no longer strand a SKU from its style. **Data patch (applied):** corrected **143** existing `ip_item_master` rows across **28** style codes (rbb0185, ptya0009, cxt0002L, PTYG0003lstdРђд) to their canonical `style_master` casing (verified 0 case-collisions first, so unambiguous). No migration. Typecheck 0 new + build green + `node --check`. User-guide ch28.

> - **PO grid: reference-grain ANCHOR (fixes mixed garment+PPK cost/sell) + on-screen off-scale size** Рђћ mixed styles (RYO0659FP jacket = garment sizes SML..XLG **and** a PPK18 pack) showed **Avg cost $0.66 / Sell $0.86 / Margin Рѕњ1278%** and a **blank** on-screen matrix (though Total $87,239.70 was right). Two fixes: (1) **grid** Рђћ `ip_item_avg_cost` (+ sell tables) store PPK costs at an **inconsistent grain**: per-PACK for a *pure* prepack style (RCB1869NBDPPK = $324) but per-EACH for a *mixed* style (RYO0659FP = $11.85 = $213.30/18). With no grain tag, `computePoLineMoney` now **anchors** to the line's own per-each cost (`poPrice ├и ppk`, grain known): whichever of {std, std├иppk} is closer is the per-each std, and that grain decision is applied to SELL too (no std Рєњ structural fallback on a `PPK` style_code). Fixes **both** directions Рђћ pure-PPK $324Рєњ$5.40 (was reading $324/each) and mixed $11.85 stays $11.85 (was $0.66). Result: P001068/P001163 Avg cost **$11.85**, Sell **$15.50**, margin ~23%. (2) **on-screen** Рђћ `LineMatrixBody` size columns now include any **ordered size the scale doesn't carry** (the PPK18 token), so the modal matrix shows the packs instead of a blank grid (mirrors the #1630 document fix; prepack-defined styles use the pack column anyway). Files: `api/_handlers/internal/purchase-orders/index.js` (+`__tests__/po-line-money.test.js`, now **10 tests**), `src/tanda/LineMatrixBody.tsx`. No migration. Typecheck 0 new + build green + 10/10 tests + live-prod SQL. User-guide ch28.

> - **PO document (View Рєњ PDF/Excel): off-scale PPK pack size no longer drops the qty** Рђћ two POs (ROF-P001163 / -P001068) exported with **Qty 0 / $0** although the grid showed them correct (~$85РђЊ87k). Cause: the styles (RYO0659FP jackets) carry **both garment sizes** (SML/MED/LRG/XLG) **and a `PPK18` pack size**, and had **no prepack definition**, so in `LineMatrixBody.getDocumentData` the size list was `payload.sizes.filter(sizesSeen)` Рђћ the intersection of the garment scale with the *ordered* PPK18 was **empty**, so no size column rendered and the packs' qty was dropped from the doc. Fix: keep the scale sizes that were ordered **plus any ordered size the scale doesn't carry** (the PPK pack token), so a sized style with prepack lines still exports its quantities. (Once a style gets a prepack definition Рђћ Style Master Рєњ Prepack matrix Рђћ `pp.pack_token` drives the column anyway; this is the safety net for styles without one.) Client-only, no API. File: `src/tanda/LineMatrixBody.tsx`. Typecheck 0 new + vite build green. User-guide ch28.

> - **PO grid: Sell grain fix (brand/customer price weighted by qty, not eaches) + 1 bad-data row** Рђћ a prepack-heavy PO (ROF-P001133) showed **Sell $65.66 / Margin 89%**. Two causes: (1) **code** Рђћ `computePoLineMoney` weighted the **brand-list / customer** sell by *eaches* while every other source weighted by *qty*; but a PPK (pack) style's brand list is **per-PACK** (the $390 list IS the pack price, like its $324 pack cost), so it read as **$390/each**. Every sell source is keyed by the line's style/SKU, whose grain matches the line's, so **all** sources now weight by **qty** (├и eaches Рєњ per-each) Рђћ no per-source exception. Fixes every PO carrying a priced PPK style (105 PPK brand-list rows at ~$390). (2) **data** Рђћ exactly one **loose** style, **RYB1416**, carried a pack price in its per-each sell (brand list **$222.90**, provisional **$217.22**); recovered to per-each ├и24 (**$9.29 / $9.05**). It's the *only* loose style with pack-grain sell data (verified). Result: P001133 Sell **$65.66 Рєњ $9.11**, margin ~21%. Files: `api/_handlers/internal/purchase-orders/index.js` (+`__tests__/po-line-money.test.js`, now **8 tests**). No migration (1-row prod data patch applied). Typecheck 0 new + build green + 8/8 tests + live-prod SQL. User-guide ch28.

> - **PO row-detail: Issued / Received / Open breakdown toggle** Рђћ the РќИ row-detail matrix gains a **Ріъ Issued / Received / Open** show/hide button (next to the Remaining/Original switch; shown when the PO has receipts). On, each colour renders **three stacked lines** per style/colour Рђћ **Issued** (original PO ordered qty, muted), **Received** (blue), **Open** (remaining to ship = ordered Рѕњ received, teal) Рђћ each with per-size cells, per-metric row + style totals, and Ext $ (ordered/received/open value). Off = the single Remaining/Original line. Reuses one per-cell accumulation (`{ordered, received, remaining}` + their $) so all views render from the same data; honours EXPLODE PPK. Client-only. File: `src/tanda/InternalPurchaseOrders.tsx`. Typecheck ratchet 0 new + vite build green. User-guide ch28.

> - **PPK prepack lines: link at import + backfill (the "Other lines" root cause)** Рђћ a PPK PO exported as CSV showed the prepacks as flat **"Other lines"** (`LAIDBACK Baggy Fit Рђд 178 @ $171.60`) separate from the style's size matrix, and the grid mis-costed them. **Root cause**: the Xoro ItemNumber for a prepack is `RYB153330PPK-Seaweed - Dark Wash-**PPK24**`, but the catalog pack SKU (`ip_item_master`) keeps the pack size in its **`size` column** and OMITS it from `sku_code` (`RYB153330PPK-SEAWEED-DARKWASH`, size `PPK24`). The import's `resolveSku` loose/expanded keys therefore missed by exactly the trailing `PPK24`, and step 3.5 explicitly skips PPK Рђћ so every prepack line imported **null-linked** (no style/size Рєњ can't join the matrix, excluded from Avg cost/PO Price). **Fix**: (1) `resolveSku` gains **step 3c** Рђћ for a PPK line, retry the loose/expanded match with the pack-size segment stripped, restricted to a family row whose own `size` is a PPK token (never binds a pack line to a loose SKU). (2) **One-time prod backfill** re-linked the **32** existing orphan prepack lines on active POs (matched by *position*: native line order Рєћ Xoro item order Рђћ validated 53/53 orphans agree on qty+description, 0 mismatches Рђћ then unique normalized sku_code; sets only `inventory_item_id`, line ids/receipts preserved). ROF-P001133: 9 "Other lines" Рєњ their `RYB1533PPK`/`RYB1619PPK`/Рђд pack SKUs (size PPK24), 0 orphans left, Avg PO Price now a clean **$7.15/each**, Total unchanged $243,336.90. Once linked, the shipped per-each grain fix (#1625) costs them correctly and they render as matrix blocks. **21** other orphans remain Рђћ their styles have **no pack SKU in the catalog** (RYB1257PPK, RYB1630BDPPK, RYO08xxРђд) Рєњ operator catalog task to create those PPK SKUs. Files: `scripts/import-xoro-orders.mjs`. No migration. `node --check` green. User-guide ch28.

> - **PO grid: PPK grain bug fixed at the root (per-each normalization in one tested helper)** Рђћ the recurring "PPK styles show ~98% margins / huge Avg cost" defect is fixed properly, not patched again. **Root cause**: every money column (Avg PO Price / Avg cost / Sell) is a `╬Б dollars ├и ╬Б eaches` **per-each** average, but a **PPK line** stores qty=**packs** + cost=**per-pack**, and the reference tables (`ip_item_avg_cost`, `recent_sell_by_style`) store PPK values **per-pack too** (a PPK60 pack's avg_cost *is* $324). Prior fixes normalised the *line-price* side (explode to eaches) but multiplied the *reference* cost/sell by **eaches** Рђћ so a $324/pack cost read as **$324/each** (├Ќ60) and Sell/Margin blended two grains (ROF-P001177: Avg cost $298.89, Sell $374.21, Margin 98.5% Рђћ all wrong; live SQL confirmed old=buggy, new=$5.55/$5.55/$6.95/~20%). **Fix**: extracted a pure, exported, **7-test** helper `computePoLineMoney(line, refs)` (`purchase-orders/index.js` + `__tests__/po-line-money.test.js`) that encodes the canonical grain rule **once** Рђћ native-grain (per-pack) cost + sales-history/std/provisional sell weight by **qty**, garment-list (customer/brand) sell weights by **eaches**, all ├и eaches. `enrichPricing` now calls it per line instead of open-coding the (drift-prone) weighting. Non-PPK POs unchanged (ppk=1). No migration. Files: `api/_handlers/internal/purchase-orders/index.js`, `+__tests__/po-line-money.test.js`. Typecheck 0 new + vite build green + 7/7 tests + `node --check` + live-prod SQL. User-guide ch28.

> - **PO grid: Avg cost PO-price fallback + Avg PO Price reordered first + row-detail unlinked-lines panel + Remaining/Original toggle** Рђћ four fixes to the native Purchase Orders grid, all off the CEO's read of the live grid. (1) **Avg cost fallback**: `enrichPricing` (`purchase-orders/index.js`) now costs each **SKU-linked** line at its **standard cost when the SKU resolves one, else the line's own PO price** Рђћ so a PO whose colorway isn't in `ip_item_avg_cost` yet (e.g. RYB1619 **SANDLOT/MELTFIELD**, whose per-unit cost is a clean $7.15 the cost table only carries under other washes) **no longer shows a blank Avg cost**; `stdDen` now equals `priceDen` for linked lines, so Avg cost is populated wherever Avg PO Price is. Fully-**unlinked** POs (Ricowell-style description-only lines) still read `Рђћ` for both (no style to price). (2) **Column order**: **Avg PO Price** now renders **immediately before Avg cost** (header, body, totals, export) Рђћ price-you-pay left of the standard benchmark. (3) **Row-detail (РќИ) unlinked panel**: only lines with a real **style + size** build the color├Ќsize matrix; SKU-less **pack/aggregate** lines (e.g. ROF-P001135's 6 PPK-prepack rows @ $171.60 = $7.15├Ќ24) are shown in a separate **"Unlinked lines"** list instead of scattering as broken single-cell rows. (4) **Remaining / Original toggle**: a partially-received PO's РќИ matrix defaults to **remaining-to-ship** qty (`ordered Рѕњ received`, floored) with a switch to **original** ordered Рђћ mirroring the **PO WIP** matrix's `itemQty` logic; ties the matrix to the grid's Remaining-to-ship column. No migration. Files: `api/_handlers/internal/purchase-orders/index.js`, `src/tanda/InternalPurchaseOrders.tsx`. Typecheck ratchet 0 new + vite build green + `node --check`. User-guide ch28.

> - **Inventory Snapshot: Avg Mrgn % column** Рђћ the Snapshot view (`InternalInventoryMatrix.tsx`) gains an **Avg Mrgn %** column placed **immediately before Avg Sale**, showing each row's gross margin = **(Avg Sale Рѕњ Avrg Cost) ├и Avg Sale** as a percent to two decimals (e.g. `42.15%`). > - **PO grid: default status + underscore-free labels + auto PO#, and a money-columns coverage BUG fixed** Рђћ (1) the PO grid **status filter now defaults to draft/issued/in-transit** (the live set) instead of All; (2) statuses render **without the underscore** (`in_transit` Рєњ *in transit*) in the filter options, grid chip and modal (raw value unchanged for filtering/API) via a `statusLabel()` helper; (3) the PO modal's **"PO number prefix" field is removed** Рђћ the number is always auto-assigned `PO-<year>-NNNNN` at issue (`nextPoNumber` already falls back to `PO`), so `po_prefix` is no longer sent. (4) РГљ **BUG**: `enrichPricing`'s `purchase_order_lines` fetch used `.in(poIds-chunk-of-200)` with **no pagination** Рєњ PostgREST's silent **1000-row cap** dropped every line past row 1000 (prod runs ~68 lines/PO Рєњ a 200-PO chunk РЅѕ13.6k lines), so **Avg PO Price / Sell / Margin were blank on most rows** though the PO carried the data (confirmed in prod: ROF-P001237 = 4 costed lines, grid blank). > - **SO missing-price warning on save** Рђћ if a style/color that carries a quantity has a **$0 Unit $**, `save()` now pops a **"Missing unit prices"** `confirmDialog` (listing each *style Рђћ color* via `listItems`) before resolving/saving. > - **SO/PO matrix fixes: per-color line PO + auto-width qty cells + SO status-filter race** Рђћ three operator fixes. (3) **SO grid status-filter race** fixed: the multi-select fires one `load()` per checkbox toggle; a slower earlier response could land last and clobber the newest filter (e.g. "cancelled only" flashing then reverting). > - **SO per-line Customer PO Рєњ auto-split into separate confirmed SOs** Рђћ the Sales Order line matrix gains a **Show line PO** toggle (next to *Show lots*/*Show images*) that reveals a **Customer PO** field on every **style line**, pre-filled with the header PO. Editing a line to a **different** PO flags it (`Рє│ splits to a new SO on save`); on save, each distinct new PO **auto-creates a new sales order** copying **all** of the source order's header info (customer, ship-to, brand, channel, dates, terms, buyer, warehouse, fulfillment, factor), carrying only the line(s) that share that PO (same-PO lines grouped onto one SO), **auto-confirmed** (SO number assigned), with the note **"Auto created due to new Customer PO."** The source order keeps the header PO + matching lines (blocked if *every* line is reassigned). A **summary dialog** lists the new SOs (number ┬и PO ┬и styles ┬и qty) with **Open** / **Open all**. No migration Рђћ each SO's PO lives on its header; the per-line tag is stripped from line payloads. `ResolvedLine.customer_po` stamped in `LineMatrixBody.resolve()`; split + child-create in `InternalSalesOrders.commitSave`. Typecheck ratchet 0 new. Files: `src/tanda/LineMatrixBody.tsx`, `src/tanda/InternalSalesOrders.tsx`. User-guide ch27.
> - **PO grid modelled on the SO grid (cost/margin strip + Avg PO Price + row explode)** Рђћ the native Purchase Orders list (`InternalPurchaseOrders.tsx` + list endpoint `enrichPricing`) is reworked to read like the Sales Orders grid. **Avg cost** now means the item's **STANDARD / catalog cost** (`ip_item_avg_cost`, keyed by SKU exactРєњloose Рђћ the same source the Inventory Snapshot + SO grid use), and a **new Avg PO Price** column carries the qty-weighted unit price on the PO's *own* lines (what it previously showed as "Avg cost"); read together they surface **PO variance** (buying above/below standard). **Margin %** and a new **Margin $** column are now `Sell Рѕњ Avg PO Price` (priced against the real buy, mirroring the SO SellРѕњCost convention; both green/red). Added a **Cancel date** column (SO parity). The **Totals** footer + **Export** gain the Avg PO Price and Margin $ figures. Each row gets a leading **РќИ carrot expander** Рєњ an inline **per-style color├Ќsize matrix** of that PO's lines with an **EXPLODE PPK** toggle (packs Рєћ units + per-each cost; shared pref with the PO/Item Matrix tab); clicking elsewhere on the row still opens the PO modal. Server margin fields (`avg_po_price_cents`, `margin_cents`, `margin_pct`) are additive. Typecheck ratchet 0 new + vite build green. > **Recent cross-cutting landings (2026-06-30)** Рђћ not tied to a single phase row:
> - **Audit Trail "Invalid or expired token" fix.** The read-only audit endpoints (`/api/internal/audit/row-history` Рђћ powering the **Audit Trail** panel in the AR/AP invoice, JE, customer/vendor/etc. detail modals Рђћ and `/api/internal/audit/log`) were the only internal-staff *read* endpoints gating on the **per-user** `authenticateCaller` (app-JWT or live Supabase session). When a user had no/expired per-user JWT Рђћ e.g. they entered Tangerine via the **#1476 PLM-session fallback** (which mints no per-user token), or past the 12h token expiry Рђћ the browser's fetch interceptor falls back to sending the **static deploy token** as the Bearer, which `authenticateCaller` rejects Рєњ **401 "Invalid or expired token"**, while every other panel worked (they use the deploy-token gate). Switched both endpoints to `authenticateInternalCaller` (the standard `INTERNAL_API_TOKEN` "is this our frontend" gate that accepts the static token via Bearer **or** `X-Internal-Token`, and fail-opens when unset) Рђћ correct for a SELECT-only surface whose rows already carry the actor. No per-user `authId` was used post-gate. Tests updated (row-history + log: 60 passing). Files: `api/_handlers/internal/audit/{row-history,log}.js`. User-guide ch06.

(**25**) The SO grid gains a **Total Margin $** column right after **Margin $** Рђћ since the server's `margin_cents` is the *per-unit* margin (`avg_sell Рѕњ avg_cost`), Total Margin $ = `margin_cents ├Ќ total_qty` (the order's full margin); added to the visible grid, the column-visibility toggle, and the Excel export. > - **Phantom on-hand recurrence fix (Inventory Matrix on-hand integrity)** Рђћ the Matrix/Snapshot On Hand is `╬Б inventory_layers.remaining_qty`, but for Xoro-sourced styles those layers were a one-time 2026-05-27 `opening_balance` seed that **Xoro sales never deplete** (`xoro-sales-sync` only writes `ip_sales_history`), so already-**sold** goods kept showing as on-hand Рђћ phantom overstatement (one-time data correction: 64 styles, 130,429 Рєњ 4,351 units). To stop it recurring, a new **nightly on-hand sync** (`api/_lib/inventory/onhand-sync.js`, hooked into `/api/planning/sync-on-hand`, env-gated by `ONHAND_LAYER_SYNC=report|apply`) rebuilds each Xoro-sourced style's on-hand layers from the **authoritative ATS feed** (`ip_inventory_snapshot` source='manual', latest date) into a dedicated `source_kind='xoro_onhand_sync'` (migration `20260929000000`). **Invariants:** acts only on SKUs in the latest feed (sold-through styles absent from the feed are left at their corrected value); manages a style **only** while every layer it has is Xoro-seeded Рђћ the moment a native event touches it (AP/PO receipt, adjustment, manufacture, transfer) or the by-size cutover (`xoro_rest_size`) owns it, the sync skips it, so it never double-counts native FIFO. Controlled rollout via `scripts/rebuild-onhand-sync.mjs --apply [--style Рђд]` (dry-run default). Dry-run scope: 771 manageable / 299 skipped of 1070 feed styles. Memory `project_phantom_opening_balance_onhand`. User-guide ch11.
> - **SO "Confirmation" button (item 7 Рђћ consolidated + buyer email default)** Рђћ the Sales Order's bottom action bar now has a single **Confirmation РќЙ** button that replaces the old separate *View* + *РюЅ Email confirmation* buttons and opens a small menu: **Download to Excel** (new `downloadOrderExcel()` in `orderDocument.ts` Рђћ an `.xlsx` of the same header + per-style color├Ќsize matrix + totals the printable doc renders, xlsx dynamically imported), **Save as PDF / Print** (the existing branded printable doc, now opened straight into the print dialog via a new `autoPrint` option), and **Email confirmation to buyerРђд** (saved orders only). The email path now **defaults the recipient to the buyer on the order** (`buyer_id`) and merges the customer's **buyers** Рђћ which carry emails, from `/api/internal/customer-buyers` Рђћ with any legacy contacts (deduped by email) so that if the order has no buyer the operator picks one from the customer master; doc-attach selection is unchanged. > - **ATS main-grid reciprocal cascade (#9, batch-G residual closed)** Рђћ the ATS grid toolbar's **Category / Sub Cat / Style / Gender** dropdowns now narrow **reciprocally**: each dropdown's options reflect the rows that pass *every other* active filter (search + the other dropdowns + store + status), so picking a Style only shows the Categories/Genders that style has, picking a Gender prunes the Styles, etc., and clearing one re-widens the others. Stale selections that fall out of scope are auto-dropped (prune effects). Previously only Sub Cat (РєљCategory) and Style (РєљCat+SubCat) cascaded one-directionally and Gender was a fixed `M/B/C/Wms/G` list. Built on the same `filterRows` predicate the grid uses, so options never diverge from results. **Scope guard:** these cascaded lists feed the **toolbar only** Рђћ the full `categories/subCategories/styles` lists passed to **Sales Comps** are left untouched so an operator can still broaden a report past the grid's current filter. Implemented in `src/ats/renderPanel.tsx` (grid* lists + prune effects) + `src/ats/panels/Toolbar.tsx` (new optional `genderOptions` prop); `src/ATS.tsx` and `filter.ts` untouched. > - **Open Tangerine from the launcher without a second login** Рђћ selecting **Tangerine ERP** from the PLM launcher (or any ­ЪДЕ Apps menu) no longer prompts the operator for a **redundant second sign-in**. Tangerine's identity is normally a Microsoft-365 token, but a launcher user authenticates once with **username/password** (written to `sessionStorage.plm_user`, cloned into the app tab on open) and previously hit Tangerine's own **"Sign in with Microsoft"** wall on top of that. Tangerine's mount auth gate now, when there is **no usable MS token**, **adopts the PLM session** (`readPlmSessionIdentity` Рєњ email/name; sets `authState=signed_in`) instead of rendering `LoginScreen`. The MS-only extras (Graph profile photo + the per-user **JWT provisioning** bridge that needs `ms_access_token`) simply stay absent until the user signs in with Microsoft Рђћ both are already **best-effort/non-fatal**, and the internal API stays gated by its own server token (`internalApiAuth` is fail-open on the static deploy token), so nothing is blocked. **Kept gated:** the standalone front door (`/login` and a cold, no-session `/tangerine`) still shows the Microsoft sign-in; the `/tangerine` **route guard** in `main.tsx` still blocks anyone explicitly set to `tangerine.access=false`. See `project_app_no_relogin_g` + `project_two_permission_systems`. Single-file change in `src/Tangerine.tsx`; user-guide ch01 (suite + Tangerine) + ch11.

> - **Inventory Snapshot Totals Рђћ per-unit explode fix + Avg Cost/Avg Sale + Wholesale rename** Рђћ the Totals strip now adds **Avg Cost** (= $ Cost ├и qty) and **Avg Sale** (= $ Wholesale ├и qty) lines per column, and the old **$ Retail** line is relabelled **$ Wholesale** (the underlying `sale_price_cents` is the SO `unit_price`, i.e. the wholesale selling price Рђћ not a retail list). Fixed the "millions" totals bug on PPK styles: `inventory-snapshot.js` exploded every qty column ├Ќunits-per-pack but left a PPK SKU's avg cost at **pack** grain (e.g. $136.80 for a 24-pack), so $ Cost = eaches ├Ќ pack-cost read 24├Ќ inflated; the handler now divides the pack cost by the same multiplier to a per-each cost ($5.70). The frontend **auto-forces per-unit explode** whenever **Totals** is on and the visible page contains any PPK style (`effectiveExplodePpk`). User-guide ch11.
> - **Style renumber + aliases (#1453)** Рђћ operators can now **renumber a style** in Style Master (e.g. drop a legacy Xoro inseam infix `RYB147730` Рєњ `RYB1477PPK`) without losing history. New `style_master.aliases text[]` (mig `20260922000000`, GIN idx, applied prod) mirrors vendors/customers.aliases. The Style Number field is **editable on edit**; on a change the PATCH **captures the old code as an alias**, **cascades the new code to `ip_item_master` (keeps `sku_code` stable)**, and **re-keys `prepack_matrices`**. All transactional history is UUID-keyed (ip_item_master.style_id, *_lines.inventory_item_id, inventory_layers.item_id, ip_sales_history_wholesale.sku_id) so it stays attached automatically; aliases cover string-grain resolvers Рђћ the **Xoro importer `loadStyles`** now indexes aliases (legacy codes still import to the renamed style) and the **prepack matcher** already bridges. ATS needs no change (resolves by stable `sku_code`). Style Master gains an **Aliases** chips field (auto-filled on renumber, hand-editable). `normalizeAliases`/`appendAlias` pure helpers +8 unit tests. User-guide ch02 + CURRENT-SCHEMA.
> - **Prepack pack entry on SO/PO (#1451)** Рђћ adding a **PPK (prepack) style** to a Sales Order or Purchase Order line matrix now renders a **pack-entry grid** (one column = the pack token, e.g. `PPK24`) instead of the garment-size grid: the operator types the **number of packs** per color (unit money **per pack**), with a **РќЙ size breakdown (explode)** toggle showing `packs ├Ќ the per-size composition` from the **Prepack Matrix master**. The order line **stores packs** (native pack grain); the size breakdown is derived (the same explode the Inventory Matrix uses). Fixes the prior dead-end where a PPK style either fell into "no size scale" (non-matrix) or rendered a full SРђЊXL grid with no pack input. Pack entry takes precedence for **any** PPK style regardless of an errant size scale; a PPK style with no matrix still accepts packs but shows a "define a matrix" hint. Additive `prepack` block on `GET /api/internal/style-matrix` (`computePrepackBlock` in `styleMatrix.js`); pure `explodePacks`/`packTotal` in `src/shared/prepack` (+unit tests); `LineMatrixBody` (shared SO/PO/AR) branches on it. User-guide ch27/28.

> **Recent cross-cutting landings (2026-06-26)** Рђћ not tied to a single phase row:
> - **Notifications now deep-link to their task across all apps (#22)** Рђћ clicking ANY notification opens the actual record it refers to instead of being inert. Two shared resolvers route every type through one place: `src/components/notifications/notificationLink.ts` for the `notifications`-table surface (**vendor bell** + **cross-app NotificationsPage**: PO WIP / Design Calendar / GS1 / Tech Packs) maps `event_type` + `metadata` (po_id/po_number/so_number/rfq_id/invoice_id/dispute_id/contract_id/Рђд) Рєњ vendor route or `/tangerine?m=Рђд&q=Рђд`; `src/tanda/notificationTarget.ts` for the Tangerine **Notification Center** (`notification_events`) maps `context_table` (sales_orders, purchase_orders, ar_invoices, invoicesРєњap, customers, vendors, gl_periods, inventory_adjustments, inventory_cycle_counts, crm_tasks, rfqs, entities) + `payload` (so_number/invoice_number) Рєњ module + drill params. Records are addressed by **human reference** (order/invoice number) Рђћ no raw UUIDs. Already-specific producer links are kept; weak links (app home, bare list) are **upgraded** from metadata; an exact record that can't be addressed **falls back to the owning module/list**; system/run events (xoro mirror runs) just mark-read. Producer link fixes: SO production-order notification now `&q=<so_number>`, vendor-quote internal notification now `/tangerine?m=rfqs` (was `/`). +14 unit tests. User-guide ch08.
> - **AI postal-code fill + postal key fix (#7)** Рђћ the address editor (`AddressFields`, used by customer billing/shipping + locations + vendors) wrote/read `postal_code`, but every Xoro-synced address stores the postal under **`postal`** (1,385 rows; 0 `postal_code`) Рђћ so synced postals never displayed. Aligned the app on **`postal`** (read `postal ?? postal_code` for legacy; write `postal`) across the editor, location summaries, and SO ship-to display. Added a **­Ъцќ** button on the postal field that calls a new `POST /api/internal/addresses/postal-suggest` (Claude Haiku) to fill the postal (US ZIP/ZIP+4 when determinable, else 5-digit) from the rest of the address; the endpoint also has a `{bulk:true}` mode that fills every customer billing/shipping + location address missing a postal (city+state present, fill-only, re-reads to avoid clobbering the concurrent sync).
> - **Customer-contact notes + reminders (#12)** Рђћ each AP/Trans/CB contact gets timestamped **notes** (author + date/time) and an optional **reminder**. New `customer_contact_notes` table (mig `20260904000000`, applied prod) keyed by a stable `id` now stamped on each `customers.contacts[]` entry (sanitizeContacts preserves it). `GET/POST/DELETE /api/internal/customer-contact-notes`; a ­ЪЊЮ Notes panel under each contact (component `CustomerContactNotes`) lists notes + adds one with an optional `datetime-local` reminder (author = current user via `getCachedAuthUserId/Name`). An hourly cron `customer-contact-reminders` finds due reminders and creates an internal `notification_event` + `notification_dispatch` for the user who set it; clicking that bell notification (`InternalNotificationCenter` now deep-links `context_table='customers'`) opens `?m=customer_master&open=<id>&contact=<id>&note=<id>` Рєњ the customer's AP/Trans/CB tab with that contact's notes open + the note highlighted. Also #11: removed the descriptive blurb from the AP/Trans/CBs tab.
> - **Customer Master Рђћ AP/Trans/CB contacts tab** Рђћ new **AP/Trans/CBs** tab holding up to **8** department contacts, each with **Department** (Accounts Payable / Transportation / Chargeback), name, email, phone (stored in the existing `customers.contacts` jsonb; backend already accepts it). The **Contact information** block (name/title/email/phone/website/WeChat) was **removed from the Details tab** (columns kept on the record, just not edited there). Row actions are now **three separate fully-framed buttons** (Scorecard / Edit / Delete) inline instead of a joined bar.
> - **Per-style returns routing (credit memos)** Рђћ customer credit memos (M23 RMA) now route each return line's revenue reversal to the style's `returns_account_id` (brand Sales Returns: 4236/4234/4235/4201) Рєњ customer `default_returns_account_id` Рєњ entity 4100, mirroring the per-style revenue/COGS routing. `buildCreditMemoLines` takes a per-item returns map; the credit-memo handler resolves it from each line's style. +unit test.
> - **Per-style GL routing** Рђћ each style now posts its sales to the GL accounts for its brand bucket (ROF Brands / Boys / PT / Private Label), matching how Xoro routes by item. New `style_master.revenue_account_id` / `cogs_account_id` / `returns_account_id` + `ar_invoice_lines.cogs_account_id` (mig `20260903000000`, applied prod). **Backfilled 1,961 of 2,100 styles** from the Xoro item GL export (`BasePartNumber` Рєњ bucket Рєњ Tangerine code; saved `scripts/backfills/xoro_gl_account_map.json` + `style_gl_from_xoro.sql`). At AR-invoice creation each line's **revenue + COGS account resolves style Рєњ customer default Рєњ entity default** ([create-invoice.js](api/_handlers/internal/sales-orders/create-invoice.js)); the `arInvoiceSent` rule now books **COGS per line** (`ln.cogs_account_id ?? invoice default`), the same way revenue was already per-line Рђћ so sales + COGS land in each brand's accounts. Unmapped styles (~139) fall back to customer/entity defaults. +unit test. Returns account is stored per style (credit-memo wiring is a follow-up). Marketplace order JE posters are separate and unchanged.
> - **Closeout-order commission (Customer Master batch 2)** Рђћ sales reps earn a different rate on closeout orders. New `customers.closeout_commission_pct` (Reps tab field) + `sales_orders.is_closeout` (a **Closeout order** checkbox on the SO header), mig `20260902000000` (applied prod). The **Customer Scorecard** commission math now splits This-Year net sales into closeout vs normal (by each invoice's SO `is_closeout`) and applies the closeout rate to the closeout portion, the rep rate to the rest; reports `closeout_sales_cents` + `closeout_commission_pct` and a blended effective `commission_pct`. Dilution apportioned proportionally.
> - **Customer Master Рђћ display polish (batch 1 of N)** Рђћ every default-* picker (brand, channel, payment terms, GL routing accounts, price list, country) now shows the **name only** (the code stays searchable) per operator request; sales-rep and factor pickers were already name-only. The **Credit limit** field is now a **comma-formatted whole-dollar** input (up to 12 digits, e.g. `1,250,000`, no decimals) instead of an 8-char decimal box. Part of a larger Customer Master batch (closeout commission, default-brand backfill, GL/postal backfills) landing across follow-up PRs.
> - **Customer Master Рђћ GL field de-dup** Рђћ removed the redundant **Default AR / Default revenue** pickers from the **Details** tab (the legacy `default_gl_ar_account_id` / `default_gl_revenue_account_id` columns, which **no posting engine ever read**). The **GL Accounts** tab (`default_ar_/revenue_/returns_/cogs_account_id` Рђћ the columns the SO line-revenue routing + AR invoice/receipt posting actually consume) is now the single source of truth. Handlers no longer write/return the legacy pair; columns kept in the DB (reversible, no migration). Prod had identical values across both families and zero legacy-only rows, so no data migration needed.

Рєњ "Ross Procurement"), not by incidental word overlap, with a one-line reason; the operator still confirms/overrides. > **Recent cross-cutting landings (2026-06-18)** Рђћ not tied to a single phase row:
> - **SO customer-PO upload Рђћ confirm-choices + duplicate guard** Рђћ the ­Ъцќ Upload customer PO flow now (1) **asks instead of guessing**: when the parsed customer didn't match exactly, or a PO colour didn't map cleanly onto a style's actual colour row, a **Confirm choices** step lets the operator pick (alongside the existing base/PPK pick) *before* the order is filled Рђћ resolved picks no longer show up as "verify"/"pick manually" lines in the after-the-fact banner. (2) **Duplicate guard**: before prefilling, the PO # is checked against existing non-cancelled SOs (`GET /api/internal/sales-orders?customer_po=` exact, case-insensitive); a hit blocks the prefill with an "already exists" warning + **Open existing SO** / **Cancel** Рђћ no duplicate SO is created. Helper gains `customerCandidates` / `matchCustomerExact` / `computeColorQuestions` / `colorPickKey` + a `colorPicks` override on `buildSeedFromResolved` (+unit tests). User-guide ch27.

> - **3PL EDI goods-receipt advice (X12 944)** Рђћ new `POST /api/internal/edi/tpl/:provider_id/receipt-advice` accepts an X12 944 (lenient `parse944`) or a structured `{po_number, lines:[{sku, qty_received}]}` / `csv`, resolves the native PO + maps each SKU to its line, logs the raw advice to `edi_messages`, and creates a **DRAFT** `tanda_po_receipts` (native path). It does NOT auto-post Рђћ the draft lands in **Receiving** for the operator to confirm + post (which books FIFO + GR/IR via the #1365 flow), so an EDI receipt keeps human confirmation. +parse944 unit tests. Applied to the `load()` of all nine report panels: Income Statement, Balance Sheet (both fetches), Trial Balance, Cash Flow, Segment P&L, GL Detail (clearing the account also invalidates in-flight loads), Sales by Customer, Sales by Rep, CRM Pipeline Report. Vitest coverage floor skipped: no coverage provider installed / no baseline, not trivially achievable.

> - **Security enforcement sprint (#1661, 2026-07-08)** Рђћ actioned the re-rate's 3/10 security finding. (1) **Financial-table RLS**: dropped the blanket `anon_all_*` FOR ALL policies on 18 ledger/AR/AP/bank/commitment tables (mig `20260964000000`) Рђћ the browser anon key can no longer read/write the GL; service-role API handlers and the entity-scoped `auth_internal_*` + vendor `vendor_own_*` policies are untouched. (2) **CORS clamp**: `api/dispatch.js` wraps `res.setHeader` so every handler's `Access-Control-Allow-Origin: *` is rewritten to an app-origin allowlist (apps.ringoffire.com, prod/preview vercel.app, localhost dev) Рђћ one central change instead of ~700 handler edits; `resolveCorsOrigin` unit-tested. (3) **Verified identity on planning endpoints**: `ip-permissions.js` now takes the caller's email from the signed app-JWT (`verifyAppJwt`) when the bridge is configured, ignoring the spoofable `x-user-email` header (dev fallback only without the secret). (4) **`RBAC_MODE=enforce` set in prod** (was `log`; both internal users verified with full effective permission sets Рђћ 113/107 rows Рђћ and enforce fails open for legacy-token callers, so zero day-one breakage). Рџа№ИЈ gotcha: `echo | vercel env add` appends `\n` and `rbacMode()` doesn't trim Рђћ use `printf`. User-guide ch24.
> - **PO "received" is now real (receipt-driven), not a fake flip** Рђћ the full P13 receivingРєњGLРєњAP 3-way-match already existed for native POs (`procurement/receipts` posts FIFO layers + the GR/IR JE `DR Inventory / CR GR/IR 2050`; `vendor-invoice-drafts` clears GR/IR via `ap_invoice_grir_match`; bookkeeper queue finalizes) Рђћ but two wires were missing: posting a receipt never rolled the native PO, and the PO modal faked "received." Fixed: `receipts/:id/post` now bumps each `purchase_order_lines.qty_received` + sets the header `received`/`in_transit`; `purchase-orders/[id]` PATCH **rejects a manual `status:'received'`**; the PO modal's fake "­ЪЊЦ Mark received" is replaced by **­ЪЊЦ Receive** Рєњ opens Receiving for that PO (`?m=receiving&po=`, which now auto-opens a new receipt). GR/IR account 2050 already existed (no new account). Рџа№ИЈ Remaining: EDI 3PL inbound Рєњ auto-create/post a receipt (manual receiving works today). User-guide ch28.
> - **PO Рюј Edit (revise an issued PO) + vendor notification** Рђћ re-opening a saved PO now shows a **Рюј Edit** button in the footer that unlocks the full header + lines for revision (ends the cancel-and-recreate workaround). **­ЪњЙ Save revision** PATCHes `{revise:true,Рђд}` (server lifts the draft-only line lock for that save) and fires a **"PO revised" notification** to the vendor's portal users (bell + email via `notifyVendor`/`vendor_users`; no-op if none). Audited via the existing T11 trigger. РюЁ Follow-up landed (#1660): revisions now apply lines as a **diff that preserves line ids** Рђћ the old delete-all+reinsert 500'd on any received PO (`tanda_po_receipt_lines` FK RESTRICT) and CASCADE-wiped `po_commitments` + `po_shipment_lines` (D3 commitments + the in-transit overlay silently vanished on every Рюј Edit); `po_commitments` are **re-derived** after a line-changing revision (kept lines refresh committed amount + status vs consumption, new lines seed `open`, removed lines drop theirs, receipt consumption stranded on a removed line re-applied oldest-first), and removing an already-received line is rejected with a 409. (The receiving Рєњ GL Рєњ AP 3-way-match rework itself shipped earlier Рђћ see P13.) User-guide ch28.

> **Recent cross-cutting landings (2026-06-13)** Рђћ not tied to a single phase row:
> - **Last-received dates synced from Xoro (nightly)** Рђћ inventory layers were all stamped with the 5/31 import date. The actual last-receipt date lives in the Playwright inventory snapshot ("Last Receipt Date"; the REST export has none). New `color_aliases` table (raw Xoro colour Рєњ canonical) + `sync_received_dates(jsonb)` RPC (migration `20260879000000`); `api/ats/upload` (which already ingests the snapshot nightly) now parses the raw CSV date (avoiding xlsx DD/MM mis-coercion), bridges the colour, and stamps the newest receipt date onto each SKU's Xoro-seeded layers. One-time backfill set 3,670 SKUs; recurs nightly.
> - **Style Master inseams auto-fill + per-inseam pack matrix** Рђћ (1) editing an existing bottoms style now **auto-fills the inseams it already sells** from its SKUs (read via `/api/internal/style-matrix`, the same set the Inventory Matrix shows) so the operator no longer has to re-type them; merged declared-first and persisted on the next Save. (2) The **­ЪЊљ Scale** (pack ratio) window becomes a **size ├Ќ inseam pack matrix** for styles that declare inseams Рђћ one pack-qty column per inseam, so each inseam carries its own size curve; pre-seeded from any existing flat pack. Storage stays backward-compatible (`size_scale_pack` is flat `{size:qty}` with no inseams, nested `{inseam:{size:qty}}` with them); the SO/PO **Qty quick-fill** resolves the matching inseam's curve per row (shared `packForInseam` in `src/shared/sizeScale.ts`, +9 unit tests). User-guide ch02/27/28.
> - **Customer style numbers on Style Master** Рђћ new `style_customer_numbers` table (migration `20260873000000`) maps one base style Рєњ each customer's own style number, so customer-customized / private-label variants stop forking a new style row per customer (the cause of the `РђдPL-COLOR-SIZE-<customer>` SKU sprawl). New `GET/POST /api/internal/style-customer-numbers` + `PATCH/DELETE /:id`; a self-managing **"Customer style numbers"** section in the Style edit modal (mirrors the Fabrics section). Reverse-lookup index for resolving a customer PO's number Рєњ base style (feeds the AI Upload-customer-PO flow + manufacturing module). User-guide ch02.
> - **Color Master normalized + NavDrawer fix** (#1288 + normalization) Рђћ registered the Color Master panel in `src/erp/modules.ts` so it actually appears under **Master Data Рєњ Color Master** (#1285 added the panel/route/mount but not the modules.ts entry that feeds the visible NavDrawer). **Normalized the colour picklist** 1,106 raw spellings Рєњ **857 canonical** (migration `20260868000000`, applied prod): case + spacing + size-leaked-into-colour + abbreviation (Lt/Dk/Hthr/Chrcl/GryРђд) folding, proper mixed-case canonical. `styleMatrix.js` now aligns declared colours to existing SKU colours case-insensitively. Рџа№ИЈ The matching **live-SKU `ip_item_master.color` rewrite is deferred** Рђћ 84% of affected rows have NULL size/inseam with size+print baked into `sku_code`; needs a structured size/inseam backfill first (see OPERATOR-TODO ­ЪЪБ).
>

> - **Color Master + declared Colors/Inseams on Style Master** (#1285) Рђћ new `color_master` table (migration `20260867000000`), **prepopulated from every distinct existing catalog colour**; new `GET/POST /api/internal/colors` + `PATCH/DELETE /:id`; standalone **Color Master panel** under Master Data Рєњ Color Master (`m=color_master`, menu key `tanda/master/colors`). Style Master gains a **Colors** multi-select (searchable chips over the master; **admins** can add a brand-new colour inline, everyone can pick existing) and an optional **Inseams** multi-value field Рђћ both stored in `style_master.attributes` (`color_ids` / `inseams`). The size-matrix lib (`api/_lib/styleMatrix.js`) now **merges declared colours + inseams into the matrix rows**, so a brand-new style (and the AI "Upload customer PO" prefill) has colour rows to fill even before any SKU exists. User-guide ch02.
>
> **Recent cross-cutting landings (2026-06-05)** Рђћ not tied to a single phase row:
> - **Allocations Workbench: per-SO Allocate/Ship/Invoice/Wave + show-all-rows fix** (#1041) Рђћ each SO sub-header now drives the whole flow in place: **Allocate** (`/allocate` RPC), **­Ъџџ Ship** (carrier/service/tracking modal Рєњ `/ship`), **­ЪДЙ Invoice** (`/create-invoice` draft), **­ЪЊд Wave** (3PL-provider modal Рєњ `/wave` EDI-940). Status-gated with tooltips. **Show-all-rows fix:** when focused on one SO via `?so=`, the GET sends `?so=&include_all=1` so the server returns **every** line of that order (bypassing `v_allocation_demand`'s terminal-line exclusion) Рђћ previously a shipped/invoiced SO looked open-only even with the filter off. `src/tanda/InternalAllocations.tsx` + `api/_handlers/internal/allocations/index.js`. User-guide ch27 updated.
> - **Carrier Master + Ship modal SearchableSelect** Рђћ `carrier_master` table pre-populated with 16 carriers (UPS/FedEx/USPS/DHL/OnTrac/LSO/Spee-Dee/Amazon/ABF/XPO/Estes/ODFL/R+L/Maersk/Evergreen/COSCO); CRUD panel under Master Data Рєњ Carriers (`/tangerine?m=carrier_master`); Ship modal carrier input replaced with SearchableSelect backed by `/api/internal/carriers`. Menu key `tanda/master/carriers`, migration `20260830000000`. User-guide ch02.
> - **HTS Master + Fabric COO/HTS AI suggest** (#1027) Рђћ `hts_master` reference table (operator-managed HTS codes + duty rates); `country_of_origin` text column on `fabric_codes`; **­Ъцќ Suggest** button on fabric edit modal calls Claude Haiku to propose top-3 HTS codes from fabric content + COO; new Master Data Рєњ ­ЪЏЃ HTS Master panel; migration `20260828000000`. User-guide ch15 updated.
> - **Inventory Matrix: SO/PO/Invoices row-views + drill-through + ATS inventory filters** (#1040) Рђћ a **Matrix / SO / PO / Invoices** view-mode switch on a picked style: SO/PO/Invoices each render a row-driven list (all statuses) of the orders/invoices containing that style, with row-click drill-through to the real Sales Orders / Purchase Orders / AR Invoices module. New read-only endpoint `GET /api/internal/style-orders?style_id=&view=` resolves item ids Рєњ header rows with customer/vendor names pre-resolved (no uuids). Also added ATS-style **Gender / Group / Category** multi-select filters that scope the style picker (`src/tanda/InternalInventoryMatrix.tsx`).
> - **Inventory Matrix: image thumbnails + brand-level view + total-cost fix** (#1022) Рђћ per-color 44px thumbnails in each row; brand-selected / no-style shows all brand styles stacked (up to 50, parallel load); `totalCostCents` now recalculated when simple-mean avg fallback fires (was showing "Рђћ").

## Operator insertions (РъЋ Рђћ ahead of the original roadmap)

These were prioritized by the operator and built out-of-sequence; they occupy the P14/P15 *slots* but are not the roadmap's original P14/P15 scope.

| РъЋ **GL rebuild closeout Рђћ `cash_je_id` re-link + durable audit/provenance record** | РюЁ COMPLETE Рђћ the two closeout items on the #1720 full-ledger rebuild. (1) **Cash-side re-link** (`stage4_cash_relink.sql`): #1720 linked only the accrual side (`accrual_je_id`) because Xoro payment txns don't carry the invoice number in their own ref. The invoice IS in the payment leg's **memo** Рђћ *Invoice Payment* Рєњ `Invoice Ref # <invoice_number>`, *Bill Payment* Рєњ `РђдBill# <invoice_number> Amount Paid Рђд`; paying JE = mirror JE whose `source_id` = the payment `txn_id`. Deterministic single-payment matches only (paid across >1 txn Рєњ left null; a single FK can't hold several payment JEs). Result **AR 8,755 / AP 3,186** `cash_je_id` linked; nulls are open/unpaid, deposit/credit-settled (non-cash), Tangerine-native, or the multi-payment set (AR 45 / AP 147). FK-only on the subledger; no GL change; idempotent. (2) **Durable provenance record** (mig `20260983000000`): the 99,160 mirror JEs were bulk-loaded with immutability/period-lock/T11 triggers disabled (CEO-approved batch) Рєњ no per-JE audit rows; provenance is `source_id`=Xoro `TxnId`. Wrote ONE approved-event row to `audit_logs` (`entity_type='gl_rebuild'`) for the bulk load + one for the cash re-link (counts, method, rollback snapshot names `je_backup_20260713`/`jel_backup_20260713`, CEO approval). ## How to update this doc

When a phase or module lands (or partially lands), in the SAME PR:
1. Flip its row status (РгюРєњ­ЪЪАРєњРюЁ) + add the PR number(s) in Refs.
2. Re-count the Summary table (done phases / 25, done modules / 49) and update the three %s.
3. Bump **Last updated**.

Keep it honest Рђћ ­ЪЪА for "arch/partial," РюЁ only when the phase is functionally shippable. The % is derived from the rows, so the rows are the source of truth.
